name:T‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçy‚ÄçX
info:Panorama Room (Double Bed) (Bathtub)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:3 Reviews
rating:2.6
posted:Posted April 16, 2024
msg:Facilities are OK, experience is terrible

It's hard to think this is a 5 star hotel
The design of the hotel room is flawed. There are no curtains on the shower room window, which causes light leakage and affects your rest.
Room soundproofing is average
The room only has a coffee table and no tables and chairs. If you need to use a computer or write, you will encounter difficulties.
When I checked in, I found a cotton swab left by the previous guest on the floor, and there were oil stains on the side of the coffee table, which gave people an unclean feeling.
At the same time, there are some problems with the air conditioning control. It needs to be adjusted to air conditioning. It takes a while for the 1st intensity to be properly cooled.
It is very convenient to contact the front desk via smart voice, but the room service is not connected to the system. After I made it clear that the light leakage would affect my rest, I was not told that I could get an eye mask at the front desk.
The design of the hotel room door is very counter-intuitive. It cannot be closed by simply closing it. It requires a second force to close the door. Sometimes other guests leave and forget to close the door, and the door will continuously sound an alarm.
The area around the hotel is being repaired, and you need to go through an overpass when going out. Because the entrance to the hotel is in a very poor location, taxis often wait on the road. However, when carrying suitcases, the huge slope at the entrance of the hotel will cause some trouble, because the ground is designed to suit It is difficult to drag the suitcase on the brick floor where the car is driven.
In addition, the hotel seemed to have no reception staff. There was no staff to help me handle my luggage when I checked in and out during working hours during the day. When I left the hotel, I almost fell down at the place where I got on the bus because of the rain and tiles.
The only thing that meets the 5-star standard is that the response speed of the front desk is okay and the robot delivers food very quickly.
The most outrageous thing is that on the last day, when there were still a few minutes left before check-out, the front desk called to urge you to check out.
It's hard to say that the hotel staff are unfriendly - they will accommodate your reasonable requests
But it is obvious that many people lack proficiency and enthusiasm for their responsibilities, which is rare in many 5-star and even 4-star hotels I have stayed in.
All in all, the experience of staying here was very average. The hotel could not even reach a satisfactory level in terms of providing the most basic rest and travel convenience.
Considering the price, location, and other hotel options, I would not recommend this hotel to anyone as their first choice
